This is a method-pack issue, not a product validation failure. |

## Manual / Diagnostic Checks

- `/map` payload baseline before the final fix: HTTP 200, `SIZE=25527457`, `TIME_TOTAL=58.320752`; React Flight contained 3521 `self.__next_f.push` chunks and full domain-list rendering.
- Phase 8.1 source check: `ProjectDailyRhythmCard` displays `今日项目任务 / 今日里程碑` in both active-project and starter states, while preserving `当前项目进度` and `继续项目`.
- Phase 8.3 source check: `ProjectMissionBrief` renders `当前任务`、`输入/输出`、`需要提交什么`、`AI 评审入口`，并把 `AI 评审入口` 说明落到现有 `保存并评审代码` action；没有新增服务端代码执行路径。
- Phase 8.4 source check: `buildProjectPortfolioItems()` emits `portfolioMarkdown` for completed projects, and `ProjectPortfolioPanel` renders `导出 Portfolio Markdown` as a read-only textarea for copying into notes, resumes, or a learning portfolio. This is read-only UI text; no DB write or server action was added.
- Phase 8.4 Portfolio Route source check: `/projects/portfolio` renders `ProjectPortfolioPageContent`, queries only completed projects scoped by `userId`, reuses `buildProjectPortfolioItems()`, and has no form/server action. `/projects` keeps the inline portfolio section and adds `打开作品集`. Focused E2E now includes this route in visual, hydration, a11y, and mobile-matrix coverage.
- Phase 2.5 source check: `buildLearningHabitGoal()` computes `周目标`、`连续学习保护` and `轻量学习模式` from existing signals; `LearningHabitGoalCard` is visible on homepage and `/progress`. This is read-only; no DB write, new table, or server action was added.
- Phase 7.1 source check: `src/server/knowledge/paths.ts` defines five guidance paths (`Agent Path`, `RAG Path`, `LLM Training Path`, `AI Industry Path`, `Benchmark Path`); `/glossary` and `/radar` no longer contain `.slice(0, 2)` in the curated path pipeline.
- Focused smoke sync check: `tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts` now checks `下周建议` with `.first()` because `/weekly` intentionally renders both an overview label and an AI-summary card title; checks Glossary path metrics with guidance-aligned `已看`; checks Review rating buttons by their actual accessible names `忘了 +1d` and `很熟 +14d`.
- Phase 7.3 page check: `/tmp/roky-radar-phase73.html` contains the four required relation-card group titles and `SWE-bench`. `LangChain` was not present for the selected local seed and is not an acceptance condition.
- Phase 7.2 page check: `/tmp/roky-home-phase72.html` contains `Roky Learn`、`今日任务` and `今日术语挑战`; it does not contain `今日人物挑战` or `今日 Benchmark 挑战` for the current local demo sample, which is expected when the current local data selects a term challenge.
- Phase 7.2 diagnostic: inline `node --import tsx -e` probes returned only default exports for some alias imports in this shell path, so the persisted-data probe was not used as evidence; product evidence is from unit/integration tests and the runtime HTML smoke.
- `/map` payload after final fix: HTTP 200, `SIZE=216442`, `TIME_TOTAL=1.791929`.
- `/admin` page check: `/tmp/roky-admin.html` contains `卡片质量审查`、`来源核验队列` and `Glossary 缺来源`.
- `/admin` Prompt Studio check: `/tmp/roky-admin-prompt-studio.html` contains `Prompt Studio`、`Prompt version`、`Schema version`、`手动 repair 测试`、`最近失败样例` and `重新生成某日期`.
- Celebration component check: `LearningCelebrationCue` renders task-specific feedback for `今日学习完成`、`复习清空`、`里程碑完成` and `误区已解决`; Today completion, Review completion, and Projects milestone completion all include the cue in targeted tests.
- Phase 4.2 Today stage status check: `getQuizStageStatus()` maps no quiz to done, zero attempts to todo, partial attempts to active, and full attempts to done; `getKnowledgeStageStatus()` maps no glossary/radar connection to done, no matched detail to todo, partial match to active, and full match to done.
- Phase 5.1 Review remediation check: `buildReviewSessionSummary()` now emits `remediationActions` whenever the session has `forgot` or `hard`; `/review` renders `补弱动作`; `/today?mode=remediation&source=review&focus=...` renders a visible remediation landing instead of silently ignoring the query.
- Phase 5.2 Mistakes repair-center check: `/mistakes` now accepts `kind` and `source=project` filters, renders a visible `类型` filter group, and exposes `生成复习卡` plus `标记已解决` actions for each mistake. The review-card action generates deterministic `mistake-card:{id}` IDs and both write actions call `assertWritableRequest()`.
- Phase 5.3 Learning Path check: `buildLearningPathSnapshot()` now aggregates quiz accuracy into stage metrics and emits `unlockCondition` plus `nextTopic`; `/path` renders `测验正确率`, `解锁条件`, and `下一步主题` in SSR HTML.
- Phase 5.4 Weekly Review check: `buildWeeklyReviewSnapshot()` now emits `weeklyOverview`, `aiSummary`, and `weeklyReportMarkdown`; `/weekly` renders `7 天总览`, Voice/Coach/project/mistake/knowledge coverage metrics, deterministic `AI 周总结`, and a readonly `导出 Weekly Markdown` report without calling AI.
- Phase 3.5 PWA shortcuts check: `manifest.webmanifest` keeps `start_url` at `/today`, exposes installation shortcuts for `今日学习`、`复习中心`、`语音反思`、`每周复盘`, and is public without login; this is metadata only and does not add service worker/offline behavior.
- Phase 10 Today full-view a11y check: `CollapsibleContentSection` keeps complete course content hidden by default, exposes button state through `aria-expanded`, links the button to the panel with `aria-controls`, and renders expanded content as a labelled `role="region"`.
- Phase 10 Progress calendar a11y check: `/progress` learning-calendar cells now expose completed/planned/none as `已完成学习`、`已安排学习`、`暂无学习记录` through `aria-label`, while preserving the existing visual color legend.
- Phase 10 FocusPlayer stage a11y check: `LearningFocusPlayer` stage-switch buttons now expose both the stage title and status in `aria-label`, so progress dots are not silent state-only controls.
- Phase 10 Shared ProgressBar a11y check: `LearningProgressBar` now exposes `role="progressbar"`, percentage value, and accessible label while preserving existing visual width behavior across Today, Review, Path, Projects, Weekly, Progress and knowledge-path surfaces.
- Phase 10 Motivation Progress Labels a11y check: Daily Quest, XP Level, Habit Goal, and Badge Shelf progress bars now pass specific Chinese `label` values into `LearningProgressBar`, so same-screen motivation progress no longer falls back to the generic `学习进度` name.
- Phase 10 Remaining Progress Labels a11y check: all remaining `src/app` and `src/components` `LearningProgressBar` call sites now pass concrete Chinese labels for Focus, Review, Path, Weekly, Map, Projects, Completion, and Knowledge Path contexts.
- Phase 10 LearningStepCard a11y check: `LearningStepCard` now exposes `第 n 步，完成/进行中/待办` through screen-reader-only text while preserving visible icons, colors, and status badges across Voice workflow surfaces.
- Phase 10 LearningTimeline a11y check: `LearningTimeline` now exposes `第 n 步，完成/进行中/待办` through screen-reader-only text while preserving visible icons, colors, and numeric order in Today full-view timelines.
- Phase 10 Knowledge Path Metric a11y check: `KnowledgePathExplorer` now keeps metric label/value visible without adding duplicate `aria-label` to noninteractive metric cards.
- Phase 10 Reduced Motion a11y check: global CSS now honors `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` by minimizing animation duration, animation iteration count, transition duration, and smooth scrolling.
- Phase 10 Shared UI a11y localization check: Dialog/Sheet close controls expose `关闭`, Breadcrumb nav exposes `面包屑导航`, and breadcrumb ellipsis exposes `更多层级` without hiding the label from assistive technology.
- Phase 6.1/6.2 Voice cleanup check: `buildVoiceTranscriptionPrompt()` now emits `Preserve these AI acronyms and technical terms.` with the full guidance term list; `normalizeVoiceTranscript()` now routes through `cleanupVoiceTranscript()` and preserves `Chain-of-Thought`, `SWE-bench`, `BM25`, `Reranker`, `Embedding`, and `Vector Database`.
- Phase 4.5 Today Completion Hub check: `LearningCompletionCard` renders `今日完成 Hub` with `生成卡片`、`小测验`、`代码提交`; `/today` supplies these metrics from existing card count, quiz attempts, and code submission state.
- Phase 4.5 Voice Reflection Recommendation check: `buildTodayCompletionNextActions()` emits `recommendedVoiceReflection` after completed plans, and `LearningCompletionCard` renders `推荐语音反思` with a `60 秒` prompt and `/voice?lessonId=...&mode=daily_understanding` link.
- Phase 8.2 Today completion project check: `LearningCompletionCard` renders `下一步：把今天的知识用到项目里` and `推荐项目任务` for both active project milestone and no-active-project starter paths, while preserving `今日项目任务` and existing `/projects` links.
- Today stage guidance check: `LearningFocusPlayer` renders `你现在要做什么`、`为什么做这个` and `完成标准`; `/today` supplies task-specific guidance for goal, lesson, guided, code, quiz, knowledge, and reflection stages.
- Mobile Today sticky check: `LearningFocusPlayer` renders `sticky top-0`, `sticky bottom-16`, and `min-h-11` for mobile progress and next-step controls.
- Mobile Review controls check: `ReviewTrainer` keeps the active card centered with `mx-auto grid w-full max-w-2xl`; `显示答案` uses `min-h-12 w-full sm:w-auto`; `ReviewRatingControls` uses mobile single-column large buttons, desktop four columns, and hides the keyboard shortcut hint below `sm`.
- Mobile Voice controls check: `VoiceCapture` renders `一键录音` and `停止并转写` with `min-h-12 w-full sm:w-auto`; browser recording stop calls the existing transcription flow directly, and `VoiceLearningPipeline` renders mobile `grid gap-2 sm:flex sm:flex-wrap` with `min-h-11 w-full sm:w-auto` CTA buttons.
- Phase E Voice Page CTA check: `/voice` page-level `打开 Coach` and right-rail learning-chain `去复习` now share `voicePageCtaClassName = "min-h-11 w-full sm:w-auto"` so mobile users do not get small header/rail CTAs while the pipeline itself is already touch-sized.
- Voice Coach handoff check: `sendVoiceNoteToCoachAction` redirects with `/coach?reviewId=...&source=voice-note&voiceNoteId=...`; `CoachVoiceSourcePanel` renders `来自 Voice Note`, mode, transcript preview, `查看 Voice Note`, and `保存为 Note` / `查看 Note`; Coach card generation continues into `/review?source=thought-review`.
- Demo data check: read-only Prisma query found no pre-existing demo-user Voice-linked `ThoughtReview`, so runtime page proof used the E2E flow to create a temporary Voice Note and delete it in `finally`.
- Mobile matrix transient diagnostic: first Phase 6.4 matrix run had one `/mistakes` 430px `page.goto` timeout after 83 passing tests; `curl /mistakes` returned HTTP 200 in `0.148938s`, the isolated Playwright test passed in `704ms`, and the complete matrix rerun passed 84/84.
- LearningMarkdown course-block check: blockquotes starting with `核心直觉`、`常见误区`、`例子/示例`、`图示/概念图/视觉化`、`互动实验/小实验/动手试试` and `自测` render as typed callouts; fenced code blocks render a `复制代码` button with `data-copy-code="true"`.
- Daily prompt check: `DAILY_PLAN_PROMPT_VERSION` is now `daily-plan-v2.10-code-sketch-course-blocks`; `buildDailyPlanMessages()` requires `lesson.contentMarkdown` to include the course-block protocol, including `> 重点` for the one idea the learner must remember, `> 例子卡` for a compact example or analogy, `> 代码/伪代码` for the minimal algorithm shape, `> 图示` for a simple visual layout or mental diagram, `> 互动实验` for a small exploratory task, and `> 自测卡` for retrieval without notes.
- A11y script boundary: direct Chrome coverage passed with `Desktop Chrome` and `Mobile Chrome`; the aggregate `npm run e2e:a11y` command also includes WebKit projects in this environment, where the local WebKit runtime path is missing, so that failure is environmental rather than product regression evidence.
- Mobile More Sheet diagnostic from earlier slice: the sheet opens and shows 首页、知识地图、课程库、我的笔记、术语库、AI Radar、项目实践、学习进度、学习路径、每周复盘、错题误区、设置。
- Mobile More Sheet console diagnostic from earlier slice: no Radix `DialogTitle` / `Description` accessibility warning after adding `SheetTitle` and `SheetDescription`.
- Local dev HMR diagnostic from earlier slice: auth proxy excludes `_next/webpack-hmr`, avoiding local hydration/interaction failure caused by redirecting the HMR endpoint.
- A11y RED/GREEN diagnostic: first `tests/e2e/a11y.spec.ts` run exposed serious contrast issues, missing select/file input names, and prohibited `aria-label` on a non-interactive step marker. Fixes landed in design tokens and specific controls before the 28-test GREEN run.
- Computed-style diagnostic: failed contrast targets used `text-muted-foreground` as `lab(48.496 0 0)` on shallow `muted`/pastel backgrounds; light theme `--muted-foreground` was darkened and disabled button opacity raised to keep visible disabled labels readable.
- Preview RED/GREEN diagnostic: running the new test with only `E2E_PREVIEW_TOKEN` against a server without matching `PREVIEW_TOKEN` failed at Preview banner lookup, proving the test does not bypass `/preview`. With the local dev server restarted using a redacted temporary `PREVIEW_TOKEN`, all 4 write-protection checks passed.
- Hydration diagnostic: current SSR HTML for `/login?next=/today` and Playwright DOM both show hidden inputs without `style`; Playwright console produced no hydration errors. The earlier `caret-color: transparent` warning was not reproducible on the current plain dev server, so this slice adds a regression guard rather than a speculative source change.
- Aegis workspace helper diagnostic: bundle/check are currently structural-red because this project has historical Markdown-only work records and missing JSON sidecars. This is evidence packaging debt, not a product runtime failure; product validation is covered by the commands above.

## Next Step

继续时优先寻找 guidance 中仍只有弱证据的本地增强点，尤其页面/组件里仍保留的小触控输入、移动端横向 action row、英文/raw 状态泄露或没有回归保护的学习入口。生产 Preview token 只读 smoke、生产部署/服务器同步仍需用户明确确认边界。

## Resume State Hint

从 `ai-learning-platform` 根目录继续。不要从记忆单独恢复；先读本文件、`10-intent.md`、`20-checkpoint.md`，再检查 `git status`。当前 Phase E Progress Summary Internal Model Copy Localization 已完成 RED/GREEN、相关回归、覆盖扫描、本地门禁和 build；Aegis helper 仍停在既有 Markdown-only 结构债。本切片只改 `/progress` 概览卡读侧文案、源码级 UI 测试和文档，不触碰 `DailyPlan.completed` 统计口径、`ReviewLog` 计数、Prisma 查询、趋势聚合、Preview 写保护、数据库、生产/SSH/部署/密钥。继续时优先寻找下一处可本地 RED/GREEN 的小触控、raw label 或学习入口弱证据点。

## Drift Check

- Scope：仍服务 Roky Learn learning desire/mobile/learning effect 目标，当前切片减少 `/progress` 概览卡中学习者可见数据库模型名。
- Compatibility：不新增迁移，不触碰生产，不改变 `DailyPlan.completed` 统计口径、`ReviewLog` 计数、Prisma 查询、趋势聚合、Preview Mode 只读边界或数据库；只改变读侧文案、源码级测试和文档记录。
- New fallback/owner：未新增 owner、adapter 或外部 fallback；Progress 页面概览卡展示仍归 `src/app/progress/page.tsx`。
- Retirement：旧的 `以 DailyPlan.completed 为准（用户时区日期）` 和 `ReviewLog：{reviewLogsCount}` 可见模板已退役；旧词只保留在测试反向断言和历史记录文本中。
- Decision：continue; Phase E Progress Summary Internal Model Copy Localization 已完成产品级 RED/GREEN、相关回归、覆盖扫描、本地门禁和 build。Aegis helper 失败仍归类为已知结构债，下一步继续寻找 guidance 中可本地关闭的小优化点。

## Resume State Hint

从 `ai-learning-platform` 根目录继续。不要从记忆单独恢复；先读本文件、`10-intent.md`、`20-checkpoint.md`，再检查 `git status`。当前 Phase E Admin Recent Plan Link Mobile Touch Targets 已完成 RED/GREEN、相关回归和本地收尾门禁；Aegis helper 仍停在既有 Markdown-only 结构债。本切片只改 `/admin` 最近每日计划维护链接展示层、源码级 UI 测试和文档，不触碰计划治理 action、`planAuditHref()`、课程路由、Preview 写保护、数据库、生产/SSH/部署/密钥。继续时优先寻找下一处可本地 RED/GREEN 的小触控、raw label 或学习入口弱证据点。

## Drift Check

- Scope：仍服务 Roky Learn learning desire/mobile/learning effect 目标，当前切片减少 `/admin` 最近每日计划维护入口在移动端的点击摩擦。
- Compatibility：不新增迁移，不触碰生产，不改变计划治理 action、`planAuditHref()`、课程路由、筛选逻辑、Preview Mode 只读边界或数据库；只改变读侧 recent plan link class、源码级测试和文档记录。
- New fallback/owner：未新增 owner、adapter 或外部 fallback；Admin 最近计划展示仍归 `src/app/admin/page.tsx`，计划治理数据和 action owner 不变。
- Retirement：旧的最近计划 `text-xs` 纯内联下划线小触控 class 已退役；旧模板只保留在测试反向断言和历史记录文本中。
- Decision：continue; Phase E Admin Recent Plan Link Mobile Touch Targets 已完成产品级 RED/GREEN、相关回归和本地收尾门禁。Aegis helper 失败仍归类为已知结构债，下一步继续寻找 guidance 中可本地关闭的小优化点。
